  let s = String.replace s " " " "%20" in
  s

  let s = "Hello World" in

code:
 (* Write a function to replace all spaces in the given string with '%20'. *)
let replace_spaces s =
  let s = String.replace s " " " "%20" in
  s
;;
let () =
  let s = "Hello World" in
  let s = replace_spaces s in
  Printf.printf "s = \"%s\"\n" s;;
val main : unit = ();
```
